<Time>1338503054197< /Time><rate>5</rate>< Review>
This is my favorite restaurant in L.A.

Believe me when I say: absolutely the best pulled pork in Los Angeles. I used to live in the South, so I know (and stop judging me).

Shocking, right? It's really quite simple, though. They cook their pulled pork for a long time and in a light bit of sauce. Most of the other pork I've had around town is cooked perfectly but has absolutely no flavor. Why bother? Doughboys also serves the pork on a fantastic flat bread type thing with a side of sauce. Seriously amazing.

Other things to get here are the grilled cheese sandwich and tomato soup (After School Special) and the Beefy Mac & Cheese. Not for the timid. A seriously thick and delicious meal.</Review>

<Date>1453005108477</Date><user_id>108231055147099693935< /user_id><text>The southern corn pudding special is a must try. Sweet, creamy, cheesy corn pudding is paired unconventionally yet successfully with pulled pork hash, grilled onions, corn, and potatoes. The whole thing is topped with two griddle fried eggs and broiled in a cast iron skillet. I got the eggs over easy in order to mix the yolky goodness all together. The result was an orgasm in my mouth. It's the best corn pudding I have ever had. I wish I could capture the sweetness in a bottle. It's a beautiful dish that is both hearty and flavorful. Bravo, Doughboys!

Another must try is the famous red velvet cake. It's worth a try even if you're not really a dessert person (which I am not). Desserts are usually too sweet for me and overwhelm me. Even I enjoyed this light, yet luscious, tasty pastry. This is the perfect level of sweetness without being overpowering. The presentation is gorgeous as well as the flavors. Doughboys can't miss!

Doughboys has an extensive breakfast and dinner menu. I've also had the salmon eggs Benedict, which was decent. I will gladly return to try other menu items, or, I might just have to stick with the corn pudding special! Enjoy.<//text>< Pics>

<Rating>5</Rating>< review>
WHERE HAS THE WAFFLE STACK BEEN ALL MY LIFE?

So, I had to fast all day yesterday. Don't ask.

Then today, when I was able to eat, I knew exactly what I wanted: french toast or a waffle. And eggs.

I checked Yelp and Doughboys came up highly recommended, and the menu had just what I wanted, so I decided to try it.

It was a nice warm day so we sat outside and I ordered the Waffle Stack, which is a waffle with a bechamel sauce, covered in broiled cheese and topped with two fried eggs. It's kind of like if a Waffle and a Monte Cristo sandwich mated.

The waffles are so big they fill the entire plate. They're light, and lightly sweet, and you can get cherry compote to top them with as well as syrup.

My Waffle Stack was about as perfect as it could be. No, wait, it was perfect, I couldn't find anything I'd change! The waffle was lovely, the cheese was cheesy, a nice layer of ham, and the eggs were perfectly cooked to run down into the waffle. My friend got a basic waffle and fruit cup and loved it, too.

This was fantastically good (and filling), and made up for not being able to eat all yesterday. In fact, I was full until dinner!

I will SO be back!<//review>

< Text>
The thing is that the food at this place is pretty unremarkable despite the hyped up impression you get online.

The pan toast may indeed be popular as the wait staff pointed out, but that doesn't mean it's tasty. I thought that cinnamon rolls + croissants French-toastified was novel and thought a mash up of two yummies would make good eats. Not so.  I left it on the plate, and I'm not known for leaving food ... especially baked goods on the plate.

It's possible that their more normal fare would be better executed, but what's the point of going somewhere unique if not to try their specialty?

The coffee's good...I'll even say above average. But overall, I'd say it's another overblown place to eat I found online.<//Text>

<user_name>Marion Soriano</user_name>< Time>
1610574729030< /Time>
< rate>
5< /rate>
< Review>
Food : Out of all the revolving sushi bars I have been to, this restaurant possibly could have the best quality fish. Their fish is very fresh if your order it through server or the  list paper they provide you to turn in. I have not seen too many places with Escolar, so it was fantastic to see that they had this sushi/sashimi. Also, keep your eye out for their  daily deals on their hand rolls; it's definitely a steal.

Service/Environment: Their service is pretty quick. Although, due to popularity, you should expect a wait during peak hours.

Price: Price is definitely great for their sushi/sashimi. But with their price definitely expect the presentation to be just average. They charge you depending on the plate the sushi/sashimi comes in, so just be aware how much you accumulate because it does add up quickly!

Overall: Kaisen Sushi Bar has got to be my favorite revolving sushi bar. It definitely is my go to for after work dinner. It is the kind of place where you feel comfortable eating by yourself or with a group. They have incredible fresh fish and huge variety of food for a very reasonable price. Just note that its not the cleanest sushi bar around, but it definitely is worth going to!< /Review>

< Text>
Absolutely incredible value. Everything is delicious and you get much higher quality than the prices would suggest. This is a revolving sushi bar so all items are made in the kitchen and rotate around on a conveyor belt for you to select at will, with an option to place special orders. Different plates are worth different prices -  there's a guide on the wall.  You get charged based on the colors of the inevitable plate tower you build as you eat. Keep your eye on the specials of the day and order a few from there.  The sea chicken is deceptively good for something so simple.<//Text>

<Review>Kaisen is one of my favorite sushi bars in Santa Ana. The restaurant is little on the small side seating about 40 or 50 people but it's worth the wait. It's located right off Bristol and Sunflower in the Staples shopping center.

This is a rotating sushi bar with daily specials. My favorite time of the week to go is on Mondays. $1.75 for Tuna hand rolls! I have been here so many times, I know the specials for each day, kind of funny and sad. Kaisen also has everyday specials like the Salmon Skin hand roll and the Negitora roll. The best place to sit is either at booths or close to the sushi chefs because you will get you're food faster.

I have never had a problem with the food. At times, the sushi on rotating belt can look dehydrated but just order directly off the menu if you want it. The Kaisen roll is one of my favorites -- 5 piece with spicy tuna, shrimp and the rolls are huge.

Service also great. Waitresses are rotating around the restaurant, ensuring your water is full or if you need something off the menu. The prices are very affordable. Menu items range from .99 to $9 depending on what you order. Give it a go and enjoy some delicious affordable sushi!<//Review><userid>113897371292918169007< /userid><gmap_id>0x80dcdf2f29f3afcf:0xdf9dae8f8bffa9d6<//gmap_id><Response>None< /Response><user_name>Ian - Fr0wnZ</user_name>< Pictures>

< Text>
I was very excited about this place because I had heard good things. But my experience here was not great. The food itself is pretty good quality. The first round of food got to us within ten minutes. The second order never got to us even after talking to the waitress. We forgot to put our table number on our order form but immediately notified the waitress and she said she would take a look in the kitchen to see if they have it and that she would correct the problem but never returned or notified us that the issue had been resolved. My boyfriend and I sat there for twenty minutes waiting to hear something from the waitress or at least for our food to come out on the revolving bar. But nothing. The waitresses aren't attentive at all and will only come up to you if you call them over. After asking another waitress about our food she went to check the kitchen and claimed there was no order back there. We asked for the check instead. When we got the check, we were charged for a pricier item that we didn't order but paid for it because we didn't want anymore problems. During the entire meal, the only grab items that were on the conveyor belt were salmon sushi, seaweed salad, and edamame. Although we don't think they were deserving a tip, we still left one. Overall, I don't think I will return.< /Text>
